    ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/schema/dereference.ts:34:1]
 33 |      */
 34 | ,-> function dereferenceNode(node: unknown, root: JsonObject, visiting: Set<string>): unknown {
 35 | |       if (!isJsonObject(node)) return node;
 36 | |       if (Array.isArray(node)) return node.map(item => dereferenceNode(item, root, visiting));
 37 | |   
 38 | |       const ref = node.$ref;
 39 | |       if (typeof ref === "string") {
 40 | |           // Break circular references
 41 | |           if (visiting.has(ref)) return {};
 42 | |           const resolved = resolveLocalRef(ref, root);
 43 | |           if (!resolved) return node; // External ref — leave as-is
 44 | |           visiting.add(ref);
 45 | |           const inlined = dereferenceNode(resolved, root, visiting);
 46 | |           visiting.delete(ref);
 47 | |   
 48 | |           // Merge sibling keywords (e.g. description, default) from the
 49 | |           // referencing node. In draft 2020-12 these are valid alongside $ref.
 50 | |           const hasSiblings = Object.keys(node).some(k => k !== "$ref");
 51 | |           if (!hasSiblings || !isJsonObject(inlined)) return inlined;
 52 | |           const merged: JsonObject = { ...inlined };
 53 | |           for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(node)) {
 54 | |               if (key !== "$ref") merged[key] = value;
 55 | |           }
 56 | |           return merged;
 57 | |       }
 58 | |   
 59 | |       const result: JsonObject = {};
 60 | |       for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(node)) {
 61 | |           // Skip $defs/definitions — they get inlined into consumers
 62 | |           if (key === "$defs" || key === "definitions") continue;
 63 | |   
 64 | |           if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 65 | |               result[key] = value.map(item => dereferenceNode(item, root, visiting));
 66 | |           } else if (isJsonObject(value)) {
 67 | |               result[key] = dereferenceNode(value, root, visiting);
 68 | |           } else {
 69 | |               result[key] = value;
 70 | |           }
 71 | |       }
 72 | |       return result;

  4 | ,-> export function areJsonValuesEqual(left: unknown, right: unknown): boolean {
  5 | |       if (Object.is(left, right)) {
  6 | |           return true;
  7 | |       }
  8 | |       if (Array.isArray(left) || Array.isArray(right)) {
  9 | |           if (!Array.isArray(left) || !Array.isArray(right) || left.length !== right.length) {

 14 | |                   return false;
 15 | |               }
 16 | |           }
 17 | |           return true;
 18 | |       }

 20 | |           return false;
 21 | |       }

 23 | |       const rightKeys = Object.keys(right);
 24 | |       if (leftKeys.length !== rightKeys.length) {
 25 | |           return false;
 26 | |       }
 27 | |       for (const key of leftKeys) {
 28 | |           if (!(key in right) || !areJsonValuesEqual(left[key], right[key])) {

 32 | |       return true;

 113 | |       // 1. Explicit search-specific env vars

  x eslint(complexity): function `tryParseLeadingJsonContainer` has a complexity of 18. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:93:1]
  92 |     
  93 | ,-> function tryParseLeadingJsonContainer(value: string): unknown | undefined {
  94 | |       const firstChar = value[0];
  95 | |       const closingChar = firstChar === "{" ? "}" : (firstChar === "[" ? "]" : undefined);
  96 | |       if (!closingChar) return undefined;
  97 | |   
  98 | |       let depth = 0;
  99 | |       let inString = false;
 100 | |       let escaped = false;
 101 | |   
 102 | |       for (let index = 0; index < value.length; index += 1) {
 103 | |           const char = value[index];
 104 | |   
 105 | |           if (inString) {
 106 | |               if (escaped) {
 107 | |                   escaped = false;
 108 | |                   continue;
 109 | |               }
 110 | |               if (char === "\\") {
 111 | |                   escaped = true;
 112 | |                   continue;
 113 | |               }
 114 | |               if (char === '"') inString = false;
 115 | |               continue;
 116 | |           }
 117 | |   
 118 | |           if (char === '"') {
 119 | |               inString = true;
 120 | |               continue;
 121 | |           }
 122 | |   
 123 | |           if (char === firstChar) {
 124 | |               depth += 1;
 125 | |               continue;
 126 | |           }
 127 | |   
 128 | |           if (char !== closingChar) continue;
 129 | |           depth -= 1;
 130 | |           if (depth !== 0) continue;
 131 | |   
 132 | |           const prefix = value.slice(0, index + 1);
 133 | |           try {
 134 | |               return JSON.parse(prefix) as unknown;
 135 | |           } catch {
 136 | |               // LLMs sometimes emit literal `\n` or `\t` between JSON tokens
 137 | |               // (e.g. `[{...}\n]`). Convert these to real whitespace and retry.
 138 | |               const cleaned = cleanLiteralEscapes(prefix);
 139 | |               if (cleaned !== prefix) {
 140 | |                   try {
 141 | |                       return JSON.parse(cleaned) as unknown;
 142 | |                   } catch {}
 143 | |               }
 144 | |               // Try escaping raw control chars that appear inside string literals.
 145 | |               const escapedControls = escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(prefix);
 146 | |               if (escapedControls !== prefix) {
 147 | |                   try {
 148 | |                       return JSON.parse(escapedControls) as unknown;
 149 | |                   } catch {}
 150 | |               }
 151 | |               // Also try single-char healing on the extracted prefix.
 152 | |               return tryHealMalformedJson(prefix);
 153 | |           }
 154 | |       }
 155 | |   
 156 | |       return undefined;
 157 | `-> }
 158 |     
     `----

  x eslint(complexity): function `escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings` has a complexity of 14. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:210:1]
 209 |      */
 210 | ,-> function escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(value: string): string {
 211 | |       let result = "";
 212 | |       let inString = false;
 213 | |       let escaped = false;
 214 | |       let changed = false;
 215 | |       for (let i = 0; i < value.length; i += 1) {
 216 | |           const ch = value[i];
 217 | |           if (inString) {
 218 | |               if (escaped) {
 219 | |                   result += ch;
 220 | |                   escaped = false;
 221 | |                   continue;
 222 | |               }
 223 | |               if (ch === "\\") {
 224 | |                   result += ch;
 225 | |                   escaped = true;
 226 | |                   continue;
 227 | |               }
 228 | |               if (ch === '"') {
 229 | |                   result += ch;
 230 | |                   inString = false;
 231 | |                   continue;
 232 | |               }
 233 | |               const code = ch.charCodeAt(0);
 234 | |               if (code < 0x20) {
 235 | |                   changed = true;
 236 | |                   switch (ch) {
 237 | |                       case "\n":
 238 | |                           result += "\\n";
 239 | |                           break;
 240 | |                       case "\r":
 241 | |                           result += "\\r";
 242 | |                           break;
 243 | |                       case "\t":
 244 | |                           result += "\\t";
 245 | |                           break;
 246 | |                       case "\b":
 247 | |                           result += "\\b";
 248 | |                           break;
 249 | |                       case "\f":
 250 | |                           result += "\\f";
 251 | |                           break;
 252 | |                       default:
 253 | |                           result += `\\u${code.toString(16).padStart(4, "0")}`;
 254 | |                   }
 255 | |                   continue;
 256 | |               }
 257 | |               result += ch;
 258 | |               continue;
 259 | |           }
 260 | |           if (ch === '"') {
 261 | |               inString = true;
 262 | |           }
 263 | |           result += ch;
 264 | |       }
 265 | |       return changed ? result : value;
 266 | `-> }
 267 |     
     `----

  x eslint(complexity): function `tryParseJsonForTypes` has a complexity of 22. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:328:1]
 327 |      */
 328 | ,-> function tryParseJsonForTypes(value: string, expectedTypes: string[]): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } {
 329 | |       const trimmed = value.trim();
 330 | |       if (!trimmed) return { value, changed: false };
 331 | |   
 332 | |       const numberCoercion = tryParseNumberString(trimmed, expectedTypes);
 333 | |       if (numberCoercion.changed) {
 334 | |           return numberCoercion;
 335 | |       }
 336 | |   
 337 | |       // Quick syntactic checks to avoid unnecessary parse attempts
 338 | |       const looksJsonObject = trimmed.startsWith("{");
 339 | |       const looksJsonArray = trimmed.startsWith("[");
 340 | |       const looksJsonLiteral =
 341 | |           trimmed === "true" || trimmed === "false" || trimmed === "null" || JSON_NUMBER_PATTERN.test(trimmed);
 342 | |   
 343 | |       if (!looksJsonObject && !looksJsonArray && !looksJsonLiteral) {
 344 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 345 | |       }
 346 | |   
 347 | |       try {
 348 | |           const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed) as unknown;
 349 | |           // If the string was "null", we parsed it to actual null.
 350 | |           // Accept this even if null isn't in expectedTypes - the LLM meant "no value".
 351 | |           // normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema will strip it from optional fields, and
 352 | |           // AJV will correctly error on required fields.
 353 | |           if (parsed === null && trimmed === "null") {
 354 | |               return { value: null, changed: true };
 355 | |           }
 356 | |           // For non-null values, only accept if the parsed type matches what the schema expects
 357 | |           if (matchesExpectedType(parsed, expectedTypes)) {
 358 | |               return { value: parsed, changed: true };
 359 | |           }
 360 | |       } catch {
 361 | |           if (looksJsonObject || looksJsonArray) {
 362 | |               // Try escaping raw control chars inside string literals (LLMs sometimes
 363 | |               // emit literal newlines/tabs inside string content rather than `\n`/`\t`).
 364 | |               const escapedControls = escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(trimmed);
 365 | |               if (escapedControls !== trimmed) {
 366 | |                   try {
 367 | |                       const parsed = JSON.parse(escapedControls) as unknown;
 368 | |                       if (matchesExpectedType(parsed, expectedTypes)) {
 369 | |                           return { value: parsed, changed: true };
 370 | |                       }
 371 | |                   } catch {}
 372 | |               }
 373 | |               // Try extracting a valid JSON prefix (handles trailing junk after balanced container)
 374 | |               const leading = tryParseLeadingJsonContainer(trimmed);
 375 | |               if (leading !== undefined && matchesExpectedType(leading, expectedTypes)) {
 376 | |                   return { value: leading, changed: true };
 377 | |               }
 378 | |               // Try healing single-character bracket errors near the end of the string
 379 | |               const healed = tryHealMalformedJson(trimmed);
 380 | |               if (healed !== undefined && matchesExpectedType(healed, expectedTypes)) {
 381 | |                   return { value: healed, changed: true };
 382 | |               }
 383 | |           }
 384 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 385 | |       }
 386 | |   
 387 | |       return { value, changed: false };
 388 | `-> }
 389 |     
     `----

  x eslint(complexity): function `normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema` has a complexity of 44. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:472:1]
 471 |     
 472 | ,-> function normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(schema: unknown, value: unknown): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } {
 473 | |       if (value === null || value === undefined) return { value, changed: false };
 474 | |       if (schema === null || typeof schema !== "object") return { value, changed: false };
 475 | |   
 476 | |       const schemaObject = schema as Record<string, unknown>;
 477 | |   
 478 | |       const normalizeAnyOfLike = (keyword: "anyOf" | "oneOf"): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } => {
 479 | |           const branches = schemaObject[keyword];
 480 | |           if (!Array.isArray(branches)) return { value, changed: false };
 481 | |   
 482 | |           let changedCandidate: { value: unknown; changed: true } | null = null;
 483 | |   
 484 | |           for (const branch of branches) {
 485 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(branch, value);
 486 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 487 | |   
 488 | |               try {
 489 | |                   const validateBranch = ajv.compile(branch);
 490 | |                   if (validateBranch(normalized.value)) {
 491 | |                       return normalized;
 492 | |                   }
 493 | |               } catch {
 494 | |                   // Ignore branch-level compilation/validation errors and keep scanning.
 495 | |               }
 496 | |   
 497 | |               if (!changedCandidate) {
 498 | |                   changedCandidate = { value: normalized.value, changed: true };
 499 | |               }
 500 | |           }
 501 | |   
 502 | |           return changedCandidate ?? { value, changed: false };
 503 | |       };
 504 | |   
 505 | |       const anyOfNormalization = normalizeAnyOfLike("anyOf");
 506 | |       if (anyOfNormalization.changed) return anyOfNormalization;
 507 | |   
 508 | |       const oneOfNormalization = normalizeAnyOfLike("oneOf");
 509 | |       if (oneOfNormalization.changed) return oneOfNormalization;
 510 | |   
 511 | |       if (Array.isArray(schemaObject.allOf)) {
 512 | |           let changed = false;
 513 | |           let nextValue: unknown = value;
 514 | |           for (const branch of schemaObject.allOf) {
 515 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(branch, nextValue);
 516 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 517 | |               nextValue = normalized.value;
 518 | |               changed = true;
 519 | |           }
 520 | |           if (changed) return { value: nextValue, changed: true };
 521 | |       }
 522 | |   
 523 | |       if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 524 | |           const itemSchema = schemaObject.items;
 525 | |           if (itemSchema === null || typeof itemSchema !== "object" || Array.isArray(itemSchema)) {
 526 | |               return { value, changed: false };
 527 | |           }
 528 | |   
 529 | |           let changed = false;
 530 | |           let nextValue = value;
 531 | |           for (let i = 0; i < value.length; i += 1) {
 532 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(itemSchema, value[i]);
 533 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 534 | |               if (!changed) {
 535 | |                   nextValue = [...value];
 536 | |                   changed = true;
 537 | |               }
 538 | |               nextValue[i] = normalized.value;
 539 | |           }
 540 | |           return { value: changed ? nextValue : value, changed };
 541 | |       }
 542 | |   
 543 | |       // Coerce string → number/integer when the schema branch declares those types.
 544 | |       // This fixes anyOf:[{type:"number"},{type:"null"}] (i.e. Optional<number>) where
 545 | |       // AJV reports an "anyOf" error rather than a "type" error, bypassing
 546 | |       // coerceArgsFromErrors which only handles keyword:"type" errors.
 547 | |       if ((schemaObject.type === "number" || schemaObject.type === "integer") && typeof value === "string") {
 548 | |           return tryParseNumberString(value, [schemaObject.type as string]);
 549 | |       }
 550 | |   
 551 | |       if (schemaObject.type !== "object") return { value, changed: false };
 552 | |       if (typeof value !== "object" || value === null) return { value, changed: false };
 553 | |       if (Array.isArray(value)) return { value, changed: false };
 554 | |       if (schemaObject.properties === null || typeof schemaObject.properties !== "object") {
 555 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 556 | |       }
 557 | |   
 558 | |       const properties = schemaObject.properties as Record<string, unknown>;
 559 | |       const required = new Set(Array.isArray(schemaObject.required) ? (schemaObject.required as string[]) : []);
 560 | |   
 561 | |       let changed = false;
 562 | |       let nextValue = value as Record<string, unknown>;
 563 | |   
 564 | |       for (const [key, propertySchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {
 565 | |           if (!(key in nextValue)) continue;
 566 | |           const currentValue = nextValue[key];
 567 | |   
 568 | |           // Strip null and the string "null" from optional fields.
 569 | |           // The LLM sometimes outputs string "null" to mean "no value".
 570 | |           if ((currentValue === null || currentValue === "null") && !required.has(key)) {
 571 | |               if (!changed) {
 572 | |                   nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 573 | |                   changed = true;
 574 | |               }
 575 | |               delete nextValue[key];
 576 | |               continue;
 577 | |           }
 578 | |           const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(propertySchema, currentValue);
 579 | |           if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 580 | |   
 581 | |           if (!changed) {
 582 | |               nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 583 | |               changed = true;
 584 | |           }
 585 | |           nextValue[key] = normalized.value;
 586 | |       }
 587 | |   
 588 | |       // Strip unknown keys with null/"null" values when the schema forbids extras.
 589 | |       // LLMs sometimes hallucinate verbs alongside valid ones (e.g. `split: null`,
 590 | |       // `original: null`). Rejecting the entire tool call wastes a turn; treating
 591 | |       // these the same as null on known optional fields is a safer fallback. Keys
 592 | |       // with non-null unknown values are left intact so genuine schema mistakes
 593 | |       // still surface as validation errors.
 594 | |       if (schemaObject.additionalProperties === false) {
 595 | |           const knownKeys = new Set(Object.keys(properties));
 596 | |           for (const key of Object.keys(nextValue)) {
 597 | |               if (knownKeys.has(key)) continue;
 598 | |               const v = nextValue[key];
 599 | |               if (v !== null && v !== "null") continue;
 600 | |               if (!changed) {
 601 | |                   nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 602 | |                   changed = true;
 603 | |               }
 604 | |               delete nextValue[key];
 605 | |           }
 606 | |       }
 607 | |   
 608 | |       return { value: changed ? nextValue : value, changed };
 609 | `-> }
 610 |     
     `----

  x eslint(complexity): private method `buildUsageCacheIdentity` has a complexity of 27. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/auth-storage.ts:791:26]
 790 |     
 791 | ,->     #buildUsageCacheIdentity(credential: UsageCredential): string {
 792 | |           const parts: string[] = [credential.type];
 793 | |           const accountId = credential.accountId?.trim();
 794 | |           if (accountId !== null && accountId !== undefined && accountId !== "") parts.push(`account:${accountId}`);
 795 | |           const email = credential.email?.trim().toLowerCase();
 796 | |           if (email !== null && email !== undefined && email !== "") parts.push(`email:${email}`);
 797 | |           const projectId = credential.projectId?.trim();
 798 | |           if (projectId !== null && projectId !== undefined && projectId !== "") parts.push(`project:${projectId}`);
 799 | |           const enterpriseUrl = credential.enterpriseUrl?.trim().toLowerCase();
 800 | |           if (enterpriseUrl !== null && enterpriseUrl !== undefined && enterpriseUrl !== "")
 801 | |               parts.push(`enterprise:${enterpriseUrl}`);
 802 | |           // Only fall back to a secret-derived key when a stable account identifier is unavailable.
 803 | |           // Including the token hash when accountId/email are present causes cache misses on
 804 | |           // every OAuth refresh — usage data is per-account, not per-token.
 805 | |           const hasStableIdentifier = Boolean(accountId ?? email);
 806 | |           if (!hasStableIdentifier) {
 807 | |               const secret = credential.apiKey?.trim() ?? credential.refreshToken?.trim() ?? credential.accessToken?.trim();
 808 | |               if (secret !== null && secret !== undefined && secret !== "") {
 809 | |                   parts.push(`secret:${Bun.hash(secret).toString(16)}`);

 1638 | |                   return undefined;
 1639 | |               }

  241 | ,-> export class AuthStorage {
  242 | |       static readonly #defaultBackoffMs = 60_000; // Default backoff when no reset time available
  243 | |   
  244 | |       /** Provider -> credentials cache, populated from store on reload(). */
  245 | |       #data: Map<string, StoredCredential[]> = new Map();
  246 | |       #runtimeOverrides: Map<string, string> = new Map();
  247 | |       /** Tracks next credential index per provider:type key for round-robin distribution (non-session use). */
  248 | |       #providerRoundRobinIndex: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  249 | |       /** Tracks the last used credential per provider for a session (used for rate-limit switching). */
  250 | |       #sessionLastCredential: Map<string, Map<string, { type: AuthCredential["type"]; index: number }>> = new Map();
  251 | |       /** Maps provider:type -> credentialIndex -> blockedUntilMs for temporary backoff. */
  252 | |       #credentialBackoff: Map<string, Map<number, number>> = new Map();
  253 | |       #usageProviderResolver?: (provider: Provider) => UsageProvider | undefined;
  254 | |       #rankingStrategyResolver?: (provider: Provider) => CredentialRankingStrategy | undefined;
  255 | |       #usageCache: UsageCache;

  264 | |       #closed = false;

  269 | |           this.#usageProviderResolver = options.usageProviderResolver ?? resolveDefaultUsageProvider;
  270 | |           this.#rankingStrategyResolver = options.rankingStrategyResolver ?? resolveDefaultRankingStrategy;

  278 | |                   warn: (message, meta) => logger.warn(message, meta),
  279 | |               } satisfies UsageLogger);
  280 | |       }
  281 | |   
  282 | |       /**
  283 | |        * Create an AuthStorage instance backed by a AuthCredentialStore.
  284 | |        * Convenience factory for standalone use (e.g., pi-ai CLI).
  285 | |        * @param dbPath - Path to SQLite database
  286 | |        */
  287 | |       static async create(dbPath: string, options: AuthStorageOptions = {}): Promise<AuthStorage> {
  288 | |           const store = await AuthCredentialStore.open(dbPath);
  289 | |           return new AuthStorage(store, options);
  290 | |       }
  291 | |   
  292 | |       /**
  293 | |        * Close the underlying credential store.
  294 | |        *
  295 | |        * After calling this, the instance must not be reused.
  296 | |        */
  297 | |       close(): void {
  298 | |           if (this.#closed) return;
  299 | |           this.#closed = true;
  300 | |           this.#store.close();
  301 | |       }
  302 | |   
  303 | |       /**
  304 | |        * Set a runtime API key override (not persisted to disk).
  305 | |        * Used for CLI --api-key flag.
  306 | |        */
  307 | |       setRuntimeApiKey(provider: string, apiKey: string): void {
  308 | |           this.#runtimeOverrides.set(provider, apiKey);
  309 | |       }
  310 | |   
  311 | |       /**
  312 | |        * Remove a runtime API key override.

  314 | |       removeRuntimeApiKey(provider: string): void {
  315 | |           this.#runtimeOverrides.delete(provider);
  316 | |       }
  317 | |   
  318 | |       /**
  319 | |        * Set a fallback resolver for API keys not found in storage or env vars.
  320 | |        * Used for custom provider keys from models.json.
  321 | |        */
  322 | |       setFallbackResolver(resolver: (provider: string) => string | undefined): void {
  323 | |           this.#fallbackResolver = resolver;
  324 | |       }
  325 | |   
  326 | |       /**
  327 | |        * Reload credentials from storage.
  328 | |        */
  329 | |       async reload(): Promise<void> {
  330 | |           const records = this.#store.listAuthCredentials();
  331 | |           const grouped = new Map<string, StoredCredential[]>();
  332 | |           for (const record of records) {
  333 | |               const list = grouped.get(record.provider) ?? [];
  334 | |               list.push({ id: record.id, credential: record.credential });
  335 | |               grouped.set(record.provider, list);
  336 | |           }
  337 | |   
  338 | |           const dedupedGrouped = new Map<string, StoredCredential[]>();
  339 | |           for (const [provider, entries] of grouped.entries()) {
  340 | |               const deduped = this.#pruneDuplicateStoredCredentials(provider, entries);
  341 | |               if (deduped.length > 0) {
  342 | |                   dedupedGrouped.set(provider, deduped);
  343 | |               }
  344 | |           }
  345 | |           this.#data = dedupedGrouped;
  346 | |       }
  347 | |   
  348 | |       /**
  349 | |        * Gets cached credentials for a provider.
  350 | |        * @param provider - Provider name (e.g., "anthropic", "openai")
  351 | |        * @returns Array of stored credentials, empty if none exist
  352 | |        */
  353 | |       #getStoredCredentials(provider: string): StoredCredential[] {
  354 | |           return this.#data.get(provider) ?? [];
  355 | |       }
  356 | |   
  357 | |       /**
  358 | |        * Updates in-memory credential cache for a provider.
  359 | |        * Removes the provider entry entirely if credentials array is empty.
  360 | |        * @param provider - Provider name (e.g., "anthropic", "openai")
  361 | |        * @param credentials - Array of stored credentials to cache
  362 | |        */
  363 | |       #setStoredCredentials(provider: string, credentials: StoredCredential[]): void {
  364 | |           if (credentials.length === 0) {
  365 | |               this.#data.delete(provider);
  366 | |           } else {
  367 | |               this.#data.set(provider, credentials);
  368 | |           }
  369 | |       }
  370 | |   
  371 | |       #resolveOAuthDedupeIdentityKey(provider: string, credential: OAuthCredential): string | null {
  372 | |           return resolveCredentialIdentityKey(provider, credential);
  373 | |       }
  374 | |   
  375 | |       #dedupeOAuthCredentials(provider: string, credentials: AuthCredential[]): AuthCredential[] {
  376 | |           const seen = new Set<string>();
  377 | |           const deduped: AuthCredential[] = [];
  378 | |           for (let index = credentials.length - 1; index >= 0; index -= 1) {
  379 | |               const credential = credentials[index];
  380 | |               if (credential.type !== "oauth") {
  381 | |                   deduped.push(credential);
  382 | |                   continue;
  383 | |               }
  384 | |               const identityKey = this.#resolveOAuthDedupeIdentityKey(provider, credential);
  385 | |               if (identityKey === null || identityKey === undefined || identityKey === "") {
  386 | |                   deduped.push(credential);
  387 | |                   continue;
  388 | |               }
  389 | |               if (seen.has(identityKey)) {
  390 | |                   continue;
  391 | |               }
  392 | |               seen.add(identityKey);
  393 | |               deduped.push(credential);
  394 | |           }
  395 | |           return deduped.reverse();
  396 | |       }
  397 | |   
  398 | |       #pruneDuplicateStoredCredentials(provider: string, entries: StoredCredential[]): StoredCredential[] {
  399 | |           const seen = new Set<string>();
  400 | |           const kept: StoredCredential[] = [];
  401 | |           const removed: StoredCredential[] = [];
  402 | |           for (let index = entries.length - 1; index >= 0; index -= 1) {
  403 | |               const entry = entries[index];
  404 | |               const credential = entry.credential;
  405 | |               if (credential.type !== "oauth") {
  406 | |                   kept.push(entry);
  407 | |                   continue;
  408 | |               }
  409 | |               const identityKey = this.#resolveOAuthDedupeIdentityKey(provider, credential);
  410 | |               if (identityKey === null || identityKey === undefined || identityKey === "") {
  411 | |                   kept.push(entry);
  412 | |                   continue;
  413 | |               }
  414 | |               if (seen.has(identityKey)) {
  415 | |                   removed.push(entry);
  416 | |                   continue;
  417 | |               }
  418 | |               seen.add(identityKey);
  419 | |               kept.push(entry);
  420 | |           }
  421 | |           if (removed.length > 0) {
  422 | |               for (const entry of removed) {
  423 | |                   this.#store.deleteAuthCredential(entry.id, "deduplicated duplicate credential");
  424 | |               }
  425 | |               this.#resetProviderAssignments(provider);
  426 | |           }
  427 | |           return kept.reverse();
  428 | |       }
  429 | |   
  430 | |       /** Returns all credentials for a provider as an array */
  431 | |       #getCredentialsForProvider(provider: string): AuthCredential[] {
  432 | |           return this.#getStoredCredentials(provider).map(entry => entry.credential);
  433 | |       }
  434 | |   
  435 | |       /** Composite key for round-robin tracking: "anthropic:oauth" or "openai:api_key" */
  436 | |       #getProviderTypeKey(provider: string, type: AuthCredential["type"]): string {
  437 | |           return `${provider}:${type}`;
  438 | |       }
  439 | |   
  440 | |       /**
  441 | |        * Returns next index in round-robin sequence for load distribution.
  442 | |        * Increments stored counter and wraps at total.
  443 | |        */
  444 | |       #getNextRoundRobinIndex(providerKey: string, total: number): number {
  445 | |           if (total <= 1) return 0;
  446 | |           const current = this.#providerRoundRobinIndex.get(providerKey) ?? -1;
  447 | |           const next = (current + 1) % total;
  448 | |           this.#providerRoundRobinIndex.set(providerKey, next);
  449 | |           return next;
  450 | |       }
  451 | |   
  452 | |       /**
  453 | |        * FNV-1a hash for deterministic session-to-credential mapping.
  454 | |        * Ensures the same session always starts with the same credential.
  455 | |        */
  456 | |       #getHashedIndex(sessionId: string, total: number): number {
  457 | |           if (total <= 1) return 0;
  458 | |           return Bun.hash.xxHash32(sessionId) % total;
  459 | |       }
  460 | |   
  461 | |       /**
  462 | |        * Returns credential indices in priority order for selection.
  463 | |        * With sessionId: starts from hashed index (consistent per session).
  464 | |        * Without sessionId: starts from round-robin index (load balancing).
  465 | |        * Order wraps around so all credentials are tried if earlier ones are blocked.
  466 | |        */
  467 | |       #getCredentialOrder(providerKey: string, sessionId: string | undefined, total: number): number[] {
  468 | |           if (total <= 1) return [0];
  469 | |           const start =
  470 | |               sessionId !== null && sessionId !== undefined && sessionId !== ""
  471 | |                   ? this.#getHashedIndex(sessionId, total)
  472 | |                   : this.#getNextRoundRobinIndex(providerKey, total);
  473 | |           const order: number[] = [];
  474 | |           for (let i = 0; i < total; i++) {
  475 | |               order.push((start + i) % total);
  476 | |           }
  477 | |           return order;
  478 | |       }
  479 | |   
  480 | |       /** Returns block expiry timestamp for a credential, cleaning up expired entries. */
  481 | |       #getCredentialBlockedUntil(providerKey: string, credentialIndex: number): number | undefined {
  482 | |           const backoffMap = this.#credentialBackoff.get(providerKey);
  483 | |           if (!backoffMap) return undefined;
  484 | |           const blockedUntil = backoffMap.get(credentialIndex);
  485 | |           if (blockedUntil === null || blockedUntil === undefined || blockedUntil === 0) return undefined;
  486 | |           if (blockedUntil <= Date.now()) {
  487 | |               backoffMap.delete(credentialIndex);
  488 | |               if (backoffMap.size === 0) {
  489 | |                   this.#credentialBackoff.delete(providerKey);
  490 | |               }
  491 | |               return undefined;
  492 | |           }
  493 | |           return blockedUntil;
  494 | |       }
  495 | |   
  496 | |       /** Checks if a credential is temporarily blocked due to usage limits. */
  497 | |       #isCredentialBlocked(providerKey: string, credentialIndex: number): boolean {
  498 | |           return this.#getCredentialBlockedUntil(providerKey, credentialIndex) !== undefined;
  499 | |       }
  500 | |   
  501 | |       /** Marks a credential as blocked until the specified time. */
  502 | |       #markCredentialBlocked(providerKey: string, credentialIndex: number, blockedUntilMs: number): void {
  503 | |           const backoffMap = this.#credentialBackoff.get(providerKey) ?? new Map<number, number>();
  504 | |           const existing = backoffMap.get(credentialIndex) ?? 0;
  505 | |           backoffMap.set(credentialIndex, Math.max(existing, blockedUntilMs));
  506 | |           this.#credentialBackoff.set(providerKey, backoffMap);
  507 | |       }
  508 | |   
  509 | |       /** Records which credential was used for a session (for rate-limit switching). */
  510 | |       #recordSessionCredential(
  511 | |           provider: string,
  512 | |           sessionId: string | undefined,
  513 | |           type: AuthCredential["type"],
  514 | |           index: number,
  515 | |       ): void {
  516 | |           if (sessionId === null || sessionId === undefined || sessionId === "") return;
  517 | |           const sessionMap = this.#sessionLastCredential.get(provider) ?? new Map();
  518 | |           sessionMap.set(sessionId, { type, index });
  519 | |           this.#sessionLastCredential.set(provider, sessionMap);
  520 | |       }
  521 | |   
  522 | |       /** Retrieves the last credential used by a session. */
  523 | |       #getSessionCredential(
  524 | |           provider: string,
  525 | |           sessionId: string | undefined,
  526 | |       ): { type: AuthCredential["type"]; index: number } | undefined {
  527 | |           if (sessionId === null || sessionId === undefined || sessionId === "") return undefined;
  528 | |           return this.#sessionLastCredential.get(provider)?.get(sessionId);
  529 | |       }
  530 | |   
  531 | |       /**
  532 | |        * Selects a credential of the specified type for a provider.
  533 | |        * Returns both the credential and its index in the original array (for updates/removal).
  534 | |        * Uses deterministic hashing for session stickiness and skips blocked credentials when possible.
  535 | |        */
  536 | |       #selectCredentialByType<T extends AuthCredential["type"]>(
  537 | |           provider: string,
  538 | |           type: T,
  539 | |           sessionId?: string,
  540 | |       ): { credential: Extract<AuthCredential, { type: T }>; index: number } | undefined {
  541 | |           const credentials = this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)
  542 | |               .map((credential, index) => ({ credential, index }))
  543 | |               .filter(
  544 | |                   (entry): entry is { credential: Extract<AuthCredential, { type: T }>; index: number } =>
  545 | |                       entry.credential.type === type,
  546 | |               );
  547 | |   
  548 | |           if (credentials.length === 0) return undefined;
  549 | |           if (credentials.length === 1) return credentials[0];
  550 | |   
  551 | |           const providerKey = this.#getProviderTypeKey(provider, type);
  552 | |           const order = this.#getCredentialOrder(providerKey, sessionId, credentials.length);
  553 | |           const fallback = credentials[order[0]];
  554 | |   
  555 | |           for (const idx of order) {
  556 | |               const candidate = credentials[idx];
  557 | |               if (!this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, candidate.index)) {
  558 | |                   return candidate;
  559 | |               }
  560 | |           }
  561 | |   
  562 | |           return fallback;
  563 | |       }
  564 | |   
  565 | |       /**
  566 | |        * Clears round-robin and session assignment state for a provider.
  567 | |        * Called when credentials are added/removed to prevent stale index references.
  568 | |        */
  569 | |       #resetProviderAssignments(provider: string): void {
  570 | |           for (const key of this.#providerRoundRobinIndex.keys()) {
  571 | |               if (key.startsWith(`${provider}:`)) {
  572 | |                   this.#providerRoundRobinIndex.delete(key);
  573 | |               }
  574 | |           }
  575 | |           this.#sessionLastCredential.delete(provider);
  576 | |           for (const key of this.#credentialBackoff.keys()) {
  577 | |               if (key.startsWith(`${provider}:`)) {
  578 | |                   this.#credentialBackoff.delete(key);
  579 | |               }
  580 | |           }
  581 | |       }
  582 | |   
  583 | |       /** Updates credential at index in-place (used for OAuth token refresh) */
  584 | |       #replaceCredentialAt(provider: string, index: number, credential: AuthCredential): void {
  585 | |           const entries = this.#getStoredCredentials(provider);
  586 | |           if (index < 0 || index >= entries.length) return;
  587 | |           const target = entries[index];
  588 | |           this.#store.updateAuthCredential(target.id, credential);
  589 | |           const updated = [...entries];
  590 | |           updated[index] = { id: target.id, credential };
  591 | |           this.#setStoredCredentials(provider, updated);
  592 | |       }
  593 | |   
  594 | |       /**
  595 | |        * Disables credential at index (used when OAuth refresh fails).
  596 | |        * The credential remains in the database but is excluded from active queries.
  597 | |        * Cleans up provider entry if last credential disabled.
  598 | |        */
  599 | |       #disableCredentialAt(provider: string, index: number, disabledCause: string): void {
  600 | |           const entries = this.#getStoredCredentials(provider);
  601 | |           if (index < 0 || index >= entries.length) return;
  602 | |           this.#store.deleteAuthCredential(entries[index].id, disabledCause);
  603 | |           const updated = entries.filter((_value, idx) => idx !== index);
  604 | |           this.#setStoredCredentials(provider, updated);
  605 | |           this.#resetProviderAssignments(provider);
  606 | |       }
  607 | |   
  608 | |       /**
  609 | |        * Get credential for a provider (first entry if multiple).
  610 | |        */
  611 | |       get(provider: string): AuthCredential | undefined {
  612 | |           return this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)[0];
  613 | |       }
  614 | |   
  615 | |       /**
  616 | |        * Set credential for a provider.
  617 | |        */
  618 | |       async set(provider: string, credential: AuthCredentialEntry): Promise<void> {
  619 | |           const normalized = Array.isArray(credential) ? credential : [credential];
  620 | |           const deduped = this.#dedupeOAuthCredentials(provider, normalized);
  621 | |           const stored = this.#store.replaceAuthCredentialsForProvider(provider, deduped);
  622 | |           this.#setStoredCredentials(
  623 | |               provider,
  624 | |               stored.map(record => ({ id: record.id, credential: record.credential })),
  625 | |           );
  626 | |           this.#resetProviderAssignments(provider);
  627 | |       }
  628 | |   
  629 | |       async #upsertOAuthCredential(provider: string, credential: OAuthCredential): Promise<void> {
  630 | |           const stored = this.#store.upsertAuthCredentialForProvider(provider, credential);
  631 | |           this.#setStoredCredentials(
  632 | |               provider,
  633 | |               stored.map(record => ({ id: record.id, credential: record.credential })),
  634 | |           );
  635 | |           this.#resetProviderAssignments(provider);
  636 | |       }
  637 | |   
  638 | |       /**
  639 | |        * Remove credential for a provider.
  640 | |        */
  641 | |       async remove(provider: string): Promise<void> {
  642 | |           this.#store.deleteAuthCredentialsForProvider(provider, "deleted by user");
  643 | |           this.#data.delete(provider);
  644 | |           this.#resetProviderAssignments(provider);
  645 | |       }
  646 | |   
  647 | |       /**
  648 | |        * List all providers with credentials.
  649 | |        */
  650 | |       list(): string[] {
  651 | |           return [...this.#data.keys()];
  652 | |       }
  653 | |   
  654 | |       /**
  655 | |        * Check if credentials exist for a provider in storage.
  656 | |        */
  657 | |       has(provider: string): boolean {
  658 | |           return this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider).length > 0;
  659 | |       }
  660 | |   
  661 | |       /**
  662 | |        * Check if any form of auth is configured for a provider.
  663 | |        * Unlike getApiKey(), this doesn't refresh OAuth tokens.
  664 | |        */
  665 | |       hasAuth(provider: string): boolean {
  666 | |           if (this.#runtimeOverrides.has(provider)) return true;
  667 | |           if (this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider).length > 0) return true;
  668 | |           if (getEnvApiKey(provider) !== undefined && getEnvApiKey(provider) !== "") return true;
  669 | |           if (this.#fallbackResolver?.(provider) !== undefined && this.#fallbackResolver?.(provider) !== "") return true;
  670 | |           return false;
  671 | |       }
  672 | |   
  673 | |       /**
  674 | |        * Check if OAuth credentials are configured for a provider.
  675 | |        */
  676 | |       hasOAuth(provider: string): boolean {
  677 | |           return this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider).some(credential => credential.type === "oauth");
  678 | |       }
  679 | |   
  680 | |       /**
  681 | |        * Get OAuth credentials for a provider.
  682 | |        */
  683 | |       getOAuthCredential(provider: string): OAuthCredential | undefined {
  684 | |           return this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider).find(
  685 | |               (credential): credential is OAuthCredential => credential.type === "oauth",
  686 | |           );
  687 | |       }
  688 | |   
  689 | |       /**
  690 | |        * Get all credentials.
  691 | |        */
  692 | |       getAll(): AuthStorageData {
  693 | |           const result: AuthStorageData = {};
  694 | |           for (const [provider, entries] of this.#data.entries()) {
  695 | |               const credentials = entries.map(entry => entry.credential);
  696 | |               if (credentials.length === 1) {
  697 | |                   result[provider] = credentials[0];
  698 | |               } else if (credentials.length > 1) {
  699 | |                   result[provider] = credentials;
  700 | |               }
  701 | |           }
  702 | |           return result;
  703 | |       }
  704 | |   
  705 | |       /**
  706 | |        * Login to an OAuth provider.
  707 | |        */
  708 | |       async login(
  709 | |           provider: OAuthProviderId,
  710 | |           ctrl: OAuthController & {
  711 | |               /** onAuth is required by auth-storage but optional in OAuthController */
  712 | |               onAuth: (info: { url: string; instructions?: string }) => void;
  713 | |               /** onPrompt is required for some providers (github-copilot, openai-codex) */
  714 | |               onPrompt: (prompt: { message: string; placeholder?: string }) => Promise<string>;
  715 | |           },
  716 | |       ): Promise<void> {
  717 | |           let credentials: OAuthCredentials;
  718 | |           const manualCodeInput = () => ctrl.onPrompt({ message: "Paste the authorization code (or full redirect URL):" });
  719 | |           switch (provider) {
  720 | |               case "openai-codex":
  721 | |                   credentials = await loginOpenAICodex({
  722 | |                       ...ctrl,
  723 | |                       onManualCodeInput: ctrl.onManualCodeInput ?? manualCodeInput,
  724 | |                   });
  725 | |                   break;
  726 | |               case "kimi":
  727 | |                   credentials = await loginKimi(ctrl);
  728 | |                   break;
  729 | |               case "moonshot":
  730 | |                   credentials = await loginMoonshot(ctrl);
  731 | |                   break;
  732 | |               case "zai": {
  733 | |                   const apiKey = await loginZai(ctrl);
  734 | |                   await this.set(provider, { type: "api_key", key: apiKey });
  735 | |                   return;
  736 | |               }
  737 | |               case "minimax-code": {
  738 | |                   const apiKey = await loginMiniMaxCode(ctrl);
  739 | |                   await this.set(provider, { type: "api_key", key: apiKey });
  740 | |                   return;
  741 | |               }
  742 | |               default: {
  743 | |                   const customProvider = getOAuthProvider(provider);
  744 | |                   if (customProvider === null || customProvider === undefined) {
  745 | |                       throw new Error(`Unknown OAuth provider: ${provider}`);
  746 | |                   }
  747 | |                   const customLoginResult = await customProvider.login({
  748 | |                       onAuth: info => ctrl.onAuth(info),
  749 | |                       onProgress: ctrl.onProgress,
  750 | |                       onPrompt: ctrl.onPrompt,
  751 | |                       onManualCodeInput: ctrl.onManualCodeInput ?? manualCodeInput,
  752 | |                       signal: ctrl.signal,
  753 | |                   });
  754 | |                   if (typeof customLoginResult === "string") {
  755 | |                       await this.set(provider, { type: "api_key", key: customLoginResult });
  756 | |                       return;
  757 | |                   }
  758 | |                   credentials = customLoginResult;
  759 | |                   break;
  760 | |               }
  761 | |           }
  762 | |           const newCredential: OAuthCredential = { type: "oauth", ...credentials };
  763 | |           await this.#upsertOAuthCredential(provider, newCredential);
  764 | |       }
  765 | |   
  766 | |       /**
  767 | |        * Logout from a provider.
  768 | |        */
  769 | |       async logout(provider: string): Promise<void> {
  770 | |           await this.remove(provider);
  771 | |       }
  772 | |   
  773 | |       // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  774 | |       // Usage API Integration
  775 | |       // Queries provider usage endpoints to detect rate limits before they occur.
  776 | |       // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  777 | |   
  778 | |       #buildUsageCredential(credential: OAuthCredential): UsageCredential {
  779 | |           return {
  780 | |               type: "oauth",
  781 | |               accessToken: credential.access,
  782 | |               refreshToken: credential.refresh,
  783 | |               expiresAt: credential.expires,
  784 | |               accountId: credential.accountId,
  785 | |               projectId: credential.projectId,
  786 | |               email: credential.email,
  787 | |               enterpriseUrl: credential.enterpriseUrl,
  788 | |           };
  789 | |       }
  790 | |   
  791 | |       #buildUsageCacheIdentity(credential: UsageCredential): string {
  792 | |           const parts: string[] = [credential.type];
  793 | |           const accountId = credential.accountId?.trim();
  794 | |           if (accountId !== null && accountId !== undefined && accountId !== "") parts.push(`account:${accountId}`);
  795 | |           const email = credential.email?.trim().toLowerCase();
  796 | |           if (email !== null && email !== undefined && email !== "") parts.push(`email:${email}`);
  797 | |           const projectId = credential.projectId?.trim();
  798 | |           if (projectId !== null && projectId !== undefined && projectId !== "") parts.push(`project:${projectId}`);
  799 | |           const enterpriseUrl = credential.enterpriseUrl?.trim().toLowerCase();
  800 | |           if (enterpriseUrl !== null && enterpriseUrl !== undefined && enterpriseUrl !== "")
  801 | |               parts.push(`enterprise:${enterpriseUrl}`);
  802 | |           // Only fall back to a secret-derived key when a stable account identifier is unavailable.
  803 | |           // Including the token hash when accountId/email are present causes cache misses on
  804 | |           // every OAuth refresh — usage data is per-account, not per-token.
  805 | |           const hasStableIdentifier = Boolean(accountId ?? email);
  806 | |           if (!hasStableIdentifier) {
  807 | |               const secret = credential.apiKey?.trim() ?? credential.refreshToken?.trim() ?? credential.accessToken?.trim();
  808 | |               if (secret !== null && secret !== undefined && secret !== "") {
  809 | |                   parts.push(`secret:${Bun.hash(secret).toString(16)}`);
  810 | |               } else {
  811 | |                   parts.push("anonymous");
  812 | |               }
  813 | |           }
  814 | |           return parts.join("|");
  815 | |       }
  816 | |   
  817 | |       #normalizeUsageBaseUrl(baseUrl?: string): string {
  818 | |           return baseUrl?.trim().replace(/\/+$/, "") ?? "";
  819 | |       }
  820 | |   
  821 | |       #buildUsageReportCacheKey(request: UsageRequestDescriptor): string {
  822 | |           const baseUrl = this.#normalizeUsageBaseUrl(request.baseUrl) || "default";
  823 | |           const identity = this.#buildUsageCacheIdentity(request.credential);
  824 | |           return `report:${request.provider}:${baseUrl}:${identity}`;
  825 | |       }
  826 | |   
  827 | |       #buildUsageReportsCacheKey(requests: ReadonlyArray<UsageRequestDescriptor>): string {
  828 | |           const snapshot = requests
  829 | |               .map(
  830 | |                   request =>
  831 | |                       `${request.provider}:${this.#normalizeUsageBaseUrl(request.baseUrl) || "default"}:${this.#buildUsageCacheIdentity(request.credential)}`,
  832 | |               )
  833 | |               .sort()
  834 | |               .join("\n");
  835 | |           return `reports:${Bun.hash(snapshot).toString(16)}`;
  836 | |       }
  837 | |   
  838 | |       #buildUsageRequest(provider: Provider, credential: UsageCredential, baseUrl?: string): UsageRequestDescriptor {
  839 | |           return { provider, credential, baseUrl };
  840 | |       }
  841 | |   
  842 | |       #buildUsageRequestForOauth(
  843 | |           provider: Provider,
  844 | |           credential: OAuthCredential,
  845 | |           baseUrl?: string,
  846 | |       ): UsageRequestDescriptor {
  847 | |           return this.#buildUsageRequest(provider, this.#buildUsageCredential(credential), baseUrl);
  848 | |       }
  849 | |   
  850 | |       #buildRefreshableOauthCredential(credential: UsageCredential): OAuthCredential | null {
  851 | |           if (
  852 | |               credential.accessToken === null ||
  853 | |               credential.accessToken === undefined ||
  854 | |               credential.accessToken === "" ||
  855 | |               credential.refreshToken === null ||
  856 | |               credential.refreshToken === undefined ||
  857 | |               credential.refreshToken === "" ||
  858 | |               credential.expiresAt === undefined
  859 | |           ) {
  860 | |               return null;
  861 | |           }
  862 | |           return {
  863 | |               type: "oauth",
  864 | |               access: credential.accessToken,
  865 | |               refresh: credential.refreshToken,
  866 | |               expires: credential.expiresAt,
  867 | |               accountId: credential.accountId,
  868 | |               projectId: credential.projectId,
  869 | |               email: credential.email,
  870 | |               enterpriseUrl: credential.enterpriseUrl,
  871 | |           };
  872 | |       }
  873 | |   
  874 | |       #mergeRefreshedUsageCredential(credential: UsageCredential, refreshed: OAuthCredentials): UsageCredential {
  875 | |           return {
  876 | |               ...credential,
  877 | |               accessToken: refreshed.access,
  878 | |               refreshToken: refreshed.refresh,
  879 | |               expiresAt: refreshed.expires,
  880 | |               accountId: refreshed.accountId ?? credential.accountId,
  881 | |               projectId: refreshed.projectId ?? credential.projectId,
  882 | |               email: refreshed.email ?? credential.email,
  883 | |               enterpriseUrl: refreshed.enterpriseUrl ?? credential.enterpriseUrl,
  884 | |           };
  885 | |       }
  886 | |   
  887 | |       #persistRefreshedUsageCredential(provider: Provider, previous: UsageCredential, next: UsageCredential): void {
  888 | |           const entries = this.#getStoredCredentials(provider);
  889 | |           const index = entries.findIndex(entry => {
  890 | |               if (entry.credential.type !== "oauth") return false;
  891 | |               if (
  892 | |                   previous.refreshToken !== null &&
  893 | |                   previous.refreshToken !== undefined &&
  894 | |                   previous.refreshToken !== "" &&
  895 | |                   entry.credential.refresh === previous.refreshToken
  896 | |               )
  897 | |                   return true;
  898 | |               if (
  899 | |                   previous.accessToken !== null &&
  900 | |                   previous.accessToken !== undefined &&
  901 | |                   previous.accessToken !== "" &&
  902 | |                   entry.credential.access === previous.accessToken
  903 | |               )
  904 | |                   return true;
  905 | |               return (
  906 | |                   entry.credential.accountId === previous.accountId &&
  907 | |                   entry.credential.email === previous.email &&
  908 | |                   entry.credential.projectId === previous.projectId
  909 | |               );
  910 | |           });
  911 | |           if (index === -1) return;
  912 | |           const existing = entries[index]?.credential;
  913 | |           if (existing.type !== "oauth") return;
  914 | |           this.#replaceCredentialAt(provider, index, {
  915 | |               type: "oauth",
  916 | |               access: next.accessToken ?? existing.access,
  917 | |               refresh: next.refreshToken ?? existing.refresh,
  918 | |               expires: next.expiresAt ?? existing.expires,
  919 | |               accountId: next.accountId,
  920 | |               projectId: next.projectId,
  921 | |               email: next.email,
  922 | |               enterpriseUrl: next.enterpriseUrl,
  923 | |           });
  924 | |       }
  925 | |   
  926 | |       async #fetchUsageUncached(request: UsageRequestDescriptor, timeoutMs?: number): Promise<UsageReport | null> {
  927 | |           const resolver = this.#usageProviderResolver;
  928 | |           if (!resolver) return null;
  929 | |   
  930 | |           const providerImpl = resolver(request.provider);
  931 | |           if (!providerImpl) return null;
  932 | |   
  933 | |           const timeoutSignal =
  934 | |               typeof timeoutMs === "number" && Number.isFinite(timeoutMs) && timeoutMs > 0
  935 | |                   ? AbortSignal.timeout(timeoutMs)
  936 | |                   : undefined;
  937 | |           let params: UsageRequestDescriptor & { signal?: AbortSignal } = { ...request, signal: timeoutSignal };
  938 | |   
  939 | |           if (
  940 | |               request.credential.type === "oauth" &&
  941 | |               request.credential.expiresAt !== undefined &&
  942 | |               Date.now() >= request.credential.expiresAt
  943 | |           ) {
  944 | |               const refreshableCredential = this.#buildRefreshableOauthCredential(request.credential);
  945 | |               if (refreshableCredential) {
  946 | |                   try {
  947 | |                       const refreshed = await this.#refreshOAuthCredential(request.provider, refreshableCredential);
  948 | |                       const refreshedCredential = this.#mergeRefreshedUsageCredential(request.credential, refreshed);
  949 | |                       this.#persistRefreshedUsageCredential(request.provider, request.credential, refreshedCredential);
  950 | |                       params = {
  951 | |                           ...params,
  952 | |                           credential: refreshedCredential,
  953 | |                       };
  954 | |                   } catch (error) {
  955 | |                       this.#usageLogger?.debug("Usage credential refresh failed, using original credential", {
  956 | |                           provider: request.provider,
  957 | |                           error: String(error),
  958 | |                       });
  959 | |                   }
  960 | |               }
  961 | |           }
  962 | |   
  963 | |           if (providerImpl.supports && !providerImpl.supports(params)) return null;
  964 | |   
  965 | |           try {
  966 | |               return await providerImpl.fetchUsage(params, {
  967 | |                   fetch: this.#usageFetch,
  968 | |                   logger: this.#usageLogger,
  969 | |               });
  970 | |           } catch (error) {
  971 | |               logger.debug("AuthStorage usage fetch failed", {
  972 | |                   provider: request.provider,
  973 | |                   error: String(error),
  974 | |               });
  975 | |               return null;
  976 | |           }
  977 | |       }
  978 | |   
  979 | |       async #fetchUsageCached(request: UsageRequestDescriptor, timeoutMs?: number): Promise<UsageReport | null> {
  980 | |           const cacheKey = this.#buildUsageReportCacheKey(request);
  981 | |           const now = Date.now();
  982 | |           const cached = this.#usageCache.get<UsageReport | null>(cacheKey);
  983 | |           if (cached && cached.expiresAt > now) {
  984 | |               return cached.value;
  985 | |           }
  986 | |   
  987 | |           const inFlight = this.#usageRequestInFlight.get(cacheKey);
  988 | |           if (inFlight) return inFlight;
  989 | |   
  990 | |           const promise = (async () => {
  991 | |               const report = await this.#fetchUsageUncached(request, timeoutMs);
  992 | |               if (report !== null) {
  993 | |                   this.#usageCache.set(cacheKey, { value: report, expiresAt: Date.now() + USAGE_REPORT_TTL_MS });
  994 | |                   return report;
  995 | |               }
  996 | |               return cached?.value ?? null;
  997 | |           })().finally(() => {
  998 | |               this.#usageRequestInFlight.delete(cacheKey);
  999 | |           });
 1000 | |   
 1001 | |           this.#usageRequestInFlight.set(cacheKey, promise);
 1002 | |           return promise;
 1003 | |       }
 1004 | |   
 1005 | |       #collectUsageRequests(options?: {
 1006 | |           baseUrlResolver?: (provider: Provider) => string | undefined;
 1007 | |       }): UsageRequestDescriptor[] {
 1008 | |           const resolver = this.#usageProviderResolver;
 1009 | |           if (!resolver) return [];
 1010 | |   
 1011 | |           const requests: UsageRequestDescriptor[] = [];
 1012 | |           const providers = new Set<string>([
 1013 | |               ...this.#data.keys(),
 1014 | |               ...DEFAULT_USAGE_PROVIDERS.map(provider => provider.id),
 1015 | |           ]);
 1016 | |   
 1017 | |           for (const providerId of providers) {
 1018 | |               const provider = providerId as Provider;
 1019 | |               const providerImpl = resolver(provider);
 1020 | |               if (!providerImpl) continue;
 1021 | |               const baseUrl = options?.baseUrlResolver?.(provider);
 1022 | |               let entries = this.#getStoredCredentials(providerId);
 1023 | |               if (entries.length > 0) {
 1024 | |                   const dedupedEntries = this.#pruneDuplicateStoredCredentials(providerId, entries);
 1025 | |                   if (dedupedEntries.length !== entries.length) {
 1026 | |                       this.#setStoredCredentials(providerId, dedupedEntries);
 1027 | |                   }
 1028 | |                   entries = dedupedEntries;
 1029 | |               }
 1030 | |   
 1031 | |               if (entries.length === 0) {
 1032 | |                   const runtimeKey = this.#runtimeOverrides.get(providerId);
 1033 | |                   const envKey = getEnvApiKey(providerId);
 1034 | |                   const apiKey = runtimeKey ?? envKey;
 1035 | |                   if (apiKey === null || apiKey === undefined || apiKey === "") continue;
 1036 | |                   const request = this.#buildUsageRequest(provider, { type: "api_key", apiKey }, baseUrl);
 1037 | |                   if (providerImpl.supports && !providerImpl.supports(request)) continue;
 1038 | |                   requests.push(request);
 1039 | |                   continue;
 1040 | |               }
 1041 | |   
 1042 | |               for (const entry of entries) {
 1043 | |                   const credential = entry.credential;
 1044 | |                   const request =
 1045 | |                       credential.type === "api_key"
 1046 | |                           ? this.#buildUsageRequest(provider, { type: "api_key", apiKey: credential.key }, baseUrl)
 1047 | |                           : this.#buildUsageRequestForOauth(provider, credential, baseUrl);
 1048 | |                   if (providerImpl.supports && !providerImpl.supports(request)) continue;
 1049 | |                   requests.push(request);
 1050 | |               }
 1051 | |           }
 1052 | |   
 1053 | |           return requests;
 1054 | |       }
 1055 | |   
 1056 | |       #getUsageReportMetadataValue(report: UsageReport, key: string): string | undefined {
 1057 | |           const metadata = report.metadata;
 1058 | |           if (!metadata || typeof metadata !== "object") return undefined;
 1059 | |           const value = metadata[key];
 1060 | |           return typeof value === "string" ? value.trim() : undefined;
 1061 | |       }
 1062 | |   
 1063 | |       #getUsageReportScopeAccountId(report: UsageReport): string | undefined {
 1064 | |           const ids = new Set<string>();
 1065 | |           for (const limit of report.limits) {
 1066 | |               const accountId = limit.scope.accountId?.trim();
 1067 | |               if (accountId !== null && accountId !== undefined && accountId !== "") ids.add(accountId);
 1068 | |           }
 1069 | |           if (ids.size === 1) return [...ids][0];
 1070 | |           return undefined;
 1071 | |       }
 1072 | |   
 1073 | |       #getUsageReportIdentifiers(report: UsageReport): string[] {
 1074 | |           const identifiers: string[] = [];
 1075 | |           const email = this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "email");
 1076 | |           if (email !== null && email !== undefined && email !== "") identifiers.push(`email:${email.toLowerCase()}`);
 1077 | |           if (report.provider === "openai-codex") {
 1078 | |               return identifiers.map(identifier => `${report.provider}:${identifier.toLowerCase()}`);
 1079 | |           }
 1080 | |           const accountId = this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "accountId");
 1081 | |           if (accountId !== null && accountId !== undefined && accountId !== "") identifiers.push(`account:${accountId}`);
 1082 | |           const account = this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "account");
 1083 | |           if (account !== null && account !== undefined && account !== "") identifiers.push(`account:${account}`);
 1084 | |           const user = this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "user");
 1085 | |           if (user !== null && user !== undefined && user !== "") identifiers.push(`account:${user}`);
 1086 | |           const username = this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "username");
 1087 | |           if (username !== null && username !== undefined && username !== "") identifiers.push(`account:${username}`);
 1088 | |           const scopeAccountId = this.#getUsageReportScopeAccountId(report);
 1089 | |           if (scopeAccountId !== null && scopeAccountId !== undefined && scopeAccountId !== "")
 1090 | |               identifiers.push(`account:${scopeAccountId}`);
 1091 | |           return identifiers.map(identifier => `${report.provider}:${identifier.toLowerCase()}`);
 1092 | |       }
 1093 | |   
 1094 | |       #mergeUsageReportGroup(reports: UsageReport[]): UsageReport {
 1095 | |           if (reports.length === 1) return reports[0];
 1096 | |           const sorted = [...reports].sort((a, b) => {
 1097 | |               const limitDiff = b.limits.length - a.limits.length;
 1098 | |               if (limitDiff !== 0) return limitDiff;
 1099 | |               return (b.fetchedAt ?? 0) - (a.fetchedAt ?? 0);
 1100 | |           });
 1101 | |           const base = sorted[0];
 1102 | |           const mergedLimits = [...base.limits];
 1103 | |           const limitIds = new Set(mergedLimits.map(limit => limit.id));
 1104 | |           const mergedMetadata: Record<string, unknown> = { ...base.metadata };
 1105 | |           let fetchedAt = base.fetchedAt;
 1106 | |   
 1107 | |           for (const report of sorted.slice(1)) {
 1108 | |               fetchedAt = Math.max(fetchedAt, report.fetchedAt);
 1109 | |               for (const limit of report.limits) {
 1110 | |                   if (!limitIds.has(limit.id)) {
 1111 | |                       limitIds.add(limit.id);
 1112 | |                       mergedLimits.push(limit);
 1113 | |                   }
 1114 | |               }
 1115 | |               if (report.metadata) {
 1116 | |                   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(report.metadata)) {
 1117 | |                       if (mergedMetadata[key] === undefined) {
 1118 | |                           mergedMetadata[key] = value;
 1119 | |                       }
 1120 | |                   }
 1121 | |               }
 1122 | |           }
 1123 | |   
 1124 | |           return {
 1125 | |               ...base,
 1126 | |               fetchedAt,
 1127 | |               limits: mergedLimits,
 1128 | |               metadata: Object.keys(mergedMetadata).length > 0 ? mergedMetadata : undefined,
 1129 | |           };
 1130 | |       }
 1131 | |   
 1132 | |       #dedupeUsageReports(reports: UsageReport[]): UsageReport[] {
 1133 | |           const groups: UsageReport[][] = [];
 1134 | |           const idToGroup = new Map<string, number>();
 1135 | |   
 1136 | |           for (const report of reports) {
 1137 | |               const identifiers = this.#getUsageReportIdentifiers(report);
 1138 | |               let groupIndex: number | undefined;
 1139 | |               for (const identifier of identifiers) {
 1140 | |                   const existing = idToGroup.get(identifier);
 1141 | |                   if (existing !== undefined) {
 1142 | |                       groupIndex = existing;
 1143 | |                       break;
 1144 | |                   }
 1145 | |               }
 1146 | |               if (groupIndex === undefined) {
 1147 | |                   groupIndex = groups.length;
 1148 | |                   groups.push([]);
 1149 | |               }
 1150 | |               groups[groupIndex].push(report);
 1151 | |               for (const identifier of identifiers) {
 1152 | |                   idToGroup.set(identifier, groupIndex);
 1153 | |               }
 1154 | |           }
 1155 | |   
 1156 | |           const deduped = groups.map(group => this.#mergeUsageReportGroup(group));
 1157 | |           if (deduped.length !== reports.length) {
 1158 | |               this.#usageLogger?.debug("Usage reports deduped", {
 1159 | |                   before: reports.length,
 1160 | |                   after: deduped.length,
 1161 | |               });
 1162 | |           }
 1163 | |           return deduped;
 1164 | |       }
 1165 | |   
 1166 | |       #isUsageLimitExhausted(limit: UsageLimit): boolean {
 1167 | |           if (limit.status === "exhausted") return true;
 1168 | |           const amount = limit.amount;
 1169 | |           if (amount.usedFraction !== undefined && amount.usedFraction >= 1) return true;
 1170 | |           if (amount.remainingFraction !== undefined && amount.remainingFraction <= 0) return true;
 1171 | |           if (amount.used !== undefined && amount.limit !== undefined && amount.used >= amount.limit) return true;
 1172 | |           if (amount.remaining !== undefined && amount.remaining <= 0) return true;
 1173 | |           if (amount.unit === "percent" && amount.used !== undefined && amount.used >= 100) return true;
 1174 | |           return false;
 1175 | |       }
 1176 | |   
 1177 | |       /** Returns true if usage indicates rate limit has been reached. */
 1178 | |       #isUsageLimitReached(report: UsageReport): boolean {
 1179 | |           return report.limits.some(limit => this.#isUsageLimitExhausted(limit));
 1180 | |       }
 1181 | |   
 1182 | |       /** Extracts the earliest reset timestamp from exhausted windows (in ms). */
 1183 | |       #getUsageResetAtMs(report: UsageReport, nowMs: number): number | undefined {
 1184 | |           const candidates: number[] = [];
 1185 | |           for (const limit of report.limits) {
 1186 | |               if (!this.#isUsageLimitExhausted(limit)) continue;
 1187 | |               const window = limit.window;
 1188 | |               if (
 1189 | |                   window?.resetsAt !== null &&
 1190 | |                   window?.resetsAt !== undefined &&
 1191 | |                   window?.resetsAt !== 0 &&
 1192 | |                   window.resetsAt > nowMs
 1193 | |               ) {
 1194 | |                   candidates.push(window.resetsAt);
 1195 | |               }
 1196 | |           }
 1197 | |           if (candidates.length === 0) return undefined;
 1198 | |           return Math.min(...candidates);
 1199 | |       }
 1200 | |   
 1201 | |       async #getUsageReport(
 1202 | |           provider: Provider,
 1203 | |           credential: OAuthCredential,
 1204 | |           options?: { baseUrl?: string; timeoutMs?: number },
 1205 | |       ): Promise<UsageReport | null> {
 1206 | |           return this.#fetchUsageCached(
 1207 | |               this.#buildUsageRequestForOauth(provider, credential, options?.baseUrl),
 1208 | |               options?.timeoutMs ?? this.#usageRequestTimeoutMs,
 1209 | |           );
 1210 | |       }
 1211 | |   
 1212 | |       async fetchUsageReports(options?: {
 1213 | |           baseUrlResolver?: (provider: Provider) => string | undefined;
 1214 | |       }): Promise<UsageReport[] | null> {
 1215 | |           if (!this.#usageProviderResolver) return null;
 1216 | |   
 1217 | |           const requests = this.#collectUsageRequests(options);
 1218 | |           if (requests.length === 0) return [];
 1219 | |   
 1220 | |           this.#usageLogger?.debug("Usage fetch requested", {
 1221 | |               providers: [...new Set(requests.map(request => request.provider))].sort(),
 1222 | |           });
 1223 | |   
 1224 | |           const cacheKey = this.#buildUsageReportsCacheKey(requests);
 1225 | |           const now = Date.now();
 1226 | |           const cached = this.#usageCache.get<UsageReport[]>(cacheKey);
 1227 | |           if (cached && cached.expiresAt > now) {
 1228 | |               return cached.value;
 1229 | |           }
 1230 | |   
 1231 | |           const inFlight = this.#usageReportsInFlight.get(cacheKey);
 1232 | |           if (inFlight) return inFlight;
 1233 | |   
 1234 | |           const promise = (async () => {
 1235 | |               for (const request of requests) {
 1236 | |                   this.#usageLogger?.debug("Usage fetch queued", {
 1237 | |                       provider: request.provider,
 1238 | |                       credentialType: request.credential.type,
 1239 | |                       baseUrl: request.baseUrl,
 1240 | |                       accountId: request.credential.accountId,
 1241 | |                       email: request.credential.email,
 1242 | |                   });
 1243 | |               }
 1244 | |   
 1245 | |               const results = await Promise.all(
 1246 | |                   requests.map(request => this.#fetchUsageCached(request, this.#usageRequestTimeoutMs)),
 1247 | |               );
 1248 | |               const reports = results.filter((report): report is UsageReport => report !== null);
 1249 | |               const deduped = this.#dedupeUsageReports(reports);
 1250 | |               if (deduped.length > 0) {
 1251 | |                   this.#usageCache.set(cacheKey, { value: deduped, expiresAt: Date.now() + USAGE_REPORT_TTL_MS });
 1252 | |               }
 1253 | |               const resolved = deduped.length > 0 ? deduped : (cached?.value ?? []);
 1254 | |               this.#usageLogger?.debug("Usage fetch resolved", {
 1255 | |                   reports: resolved.map(report => {
 1256 | |                       const accountLabel =
 1257 | |                           this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "email") ??
 1258 | |                           this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "accountId") ??
 1259 | |                           this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "account") ??
 1260 | |                           this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "user") ??
 1261 | |                           this.#getUsageReportMetadataValue(report, "username") ??
 1262 | |                           this.#getUsageReportScopeAccountId(report);
 1263 | |                       return {
 1264 | |                           provider: report.provider,
 1265 | |                           limits: report.limits.length,
 1266 | |                           account: accountLabel,
 1267 | |                       };
 1268 | |                   }),
 1269 | |               });
 1270 | |               return resolved;
 1271 | |           })().finally(() => {
 1272 | |               this.#usageReportsInFlight.delete(cacheKey);
 1273 | |           });
 1274 | |   
 1275 | |           this.#usageReportsInFlight.set(cacheKey, promise);
 1276 | |           return promise;
 1277 | |       }
 1278 | |   
 1279 | |       /**
 1280 | |        * Marks the current session's credential as temporarily blocked due to usage limits.
 1281 | |        * Uses usage reports to determine accurate reset time when available.
 1282 | |        * Returns true if a credential was blocked, enabling automatic fallback to the next credential.
 1283 | |        */
 1284 | |       async markUsageLimitReached(
 1285 | |           provider: string,
 1286 | |           sessionId: string | undefined,
 1287 | |           options?: { retryAfterMs?: number; baseUrl?: string },
 1288 | |       ): Promise<boolean> {
 1289 | |           const sessionCredential = this.#getSessionCredential(provider, sessionId);
 1290 | |           if (!sessionCredential) return false;
 1291 | |   
 1292 | |           const providerKey = this.#getProviderTypeKey(provider, sessionCredential.type);
 1293 | |           const now = Date.now();
 1294 | |           let blockedUntil = now + (options?.retryAfterMs ?? AuthStorage.#defaultBackoffMs);
 1295 | |   
 1296 | |           if (sessionCredential.type === "oauth" && this.#rankingStrategyResolver?.(provider)) {
 1297 | |               const credential = this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)[sessionCredential.index];
 1298 | |               if (credential?.type === "oauth") {
 1299 | |                   const report = await this.#getUsageReport(provider, credential, options);
 1300 | |                   if (report && this.#isUsageLimitReached(report)) {
 1301 | |                       const resetAtMs = this.#getUsageResetAtMs(report, Date.now());
 1302 | |                       if (resetAtMs !== null && resetAtMs !== undefined && resetAtMs !== 0 && resetAtMs > blockedUntil) {
 1303 | |                           blockedUntil = resetAtMs;
 1304 | |                       }
 1305 | |                   }
 1306 | |               }
 1307 | |           }
 1308 | |   
 1309 | |           this.#markCredentialBlocked(providerKey, sessionCredential.index, blockedUntil);
 1310 | |   
 1311 | |           const remainingCredentials = this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)
 1312 | |               .map((credential, index) => ({ credential, index }))
 1313 | |               .filter(
 1314 | |                   (entry): entry is { credential: AuthCredential; index: number } =>
 1315 | |                       entry.credential.type === sessionCredential.type && entry.index !== sessionCredential.index,
 1316 | |               );
 1317 | |   
 1318 | |           return remainingCredentials.some(candidate => !this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, candidate.index));
 1319 | |       }
 1320 | |   
 1321 | |       #resolveWindowResetAt(window: UsageLimit["window"]): number | undefined {
 1322 | |           if (!window) return undefined;
 1323 | |           if (typeof window.resetsAt === "number" && Number.isFinite(window.resetsAt)) {
 1324 | |               return window.resetsAt;
 1325 | |           }
 1326 | |           return undefined;
 1327 | |       }
 1328 | |   
 1329 | |       #normalizeUsageFraction(limit: UsageLimit | undefined): number {
 1330 | |           const usedFraction = limit?.amount.usedFraction;
 1331 | |           if (typeof usedFraction !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(usedFraction)) {
 1332 | |               return 0.5;
