 1333 | |           }
 1334 | |           return Math.min(Math.max(usedFraction, 0), 1);
 1335 | |       }
 1336 | |   
 1337 | |       /** Computes `usedFraction / elapsedHours` — consumption rate per hour within the current window. Lower drain rate = less pressure = preferred. */
 1338 | |       #computeWindowDrainRate(limit: UsageLimit | undefined, nowMs: number, fallbackDurationMs: number): number {
 1339 | |           const usedFraction = this.#normalizeUsageFraction(limit);
 1340 | |           const durationMs = limit?.window?.durationMs ?? fallbackDurationMs;
 1341 | |           if (!Number.isFinite(durationMs) || durationMs <= 0) {
 1342 | |               return usedFraction;
 1343 | |           }
 1344 | |           const resetAt = this.#resolveWindowResetAt(limit?.window);
 1345 | |           if (!Number.isFinite(resetAt)) {
 1346 | |               return usedFraction;
 1347 | |           }
 1348 | |           const remainingWindowMs = (resetAt as number) - nowMs;
 1349 | |           const clampedRemainingWindowMs = Math.min(Math.max(remainingWindowMs, 0), durationMs);
 1350 | |           const elapsedMs = durationMs - clampedRemainingWindowMs;
 1351 | |           if (elapsedMs <= 0) {
 1352 | |               return usedFraction;
 1353 | |           }
 1354 | |           const elapsedHours = elapsedMs / (60 * 60 * 1000);
 1355 | |           if (!Number.isFinite(elapsedHours) || elapsedHours <= 0) {
 1356 | |               return usedFraction;
 1357 | |           }
 1358 | |           return usedFraction / elapsedHours;
 1359 | |       }
 1360 | |   
 1361 | |       async #rankOAuthSelections(args: {
 1362 | |           providerKey: string;
 1363 | |           provider: string;
 1364 | |           order: number[];
 1365 | |           credentials: Array<{ credential: OAuthCredential; index: number }>;
 1366 | |           options?: AuthApiKeyOptions;
 1367 | |           strategy: CredentialRankingStrategy;
 1368 | |       }): Promise<
 1369 | |           Array<{
 1370 | |               selection: { credential: OAuthCredential; index: number };
 1371 | |               usage: UsageReport | null;
 1372 | |               usageChecked: boolean;
 1373 | |           }>
 1374 | |       > {
 1375 | |           const nowMs = Date.now();
 1376 | |           const { strategy } = args;
 1377 | |           const ranked: Array<{
 1378 | |               selection: { credential: OAuthCredential; index: number };
 1379 | |               usage: UsageReport | null;
 1380 | |               usageChecked: boolean;
 1381 | |               blocked: boolean;
 1382 | |               blockedUntil?: number;
 1383 | |               hasPriorityBoost: boolean;
 1384 | |               secondaryUsed: number;
 1385 | |               secondaryDrainRate: number;
 1386 | |               primaryUsed: number;
 1387 | |               primaryDrainRate: number;
 1388 | |               orderPos: number;
 1389 | |           }> = [];
 1390 | |           // Pre-fetch usage reports in parallel for non-blocked credentials
 1391 | |           const usageResults = await Promise.all(
 1392 | |               args.order.map(async idx => {
 1393 | |                   const selection = args.credentials[idx];
 1394 | |                   if (selection === undefined) return null;
 1395 | |                   const blockedUntil = this.#getCredentialBlockedUntil(args.providerKey, selection.index);
 1396 | |                   if (blockedUntil !== undefined) return { selection, usage: null, usageChecked: false, blockedUntil };
 1397 | |                   const usage = await this.#getUsageReport(args.provider, selection.credential, {
 1398 | |                       ...args.options,
 1399 | |                       timeoutMs: this.#usageRequestTimeoutMs,
 1400 | |                   });
 1401 | |                   return { selection, usage, usageChecked: true, blockedUntil: undefined as number | undefined };
 1402 | |               }),
 1403 | |           );
 1404 | |   
 1405 | |           for (let orderPos = 0; orderPos < usageResults.length; orderPos += 1) {
 1406 | |               const result = usageResults[orderPos];
 1407 | |               if (!result) continue;
 1408 | |               const { selection, usage, usageChecked } = result;
 1409 | |               let { blockedUntil } = result;
 1410 | |               let blocked = blockedUntil !== undefined;
 1411 | |               if (!blocked && usage && this.#isUsageLimitReached(usage)) {
 1412 | |                   const resetAtMs = this.#getUsageResetAtMs(usage, nowMs);
 1413 | |                   blockedUntil = resetAtMs ?? Date.now() + AuthStorage.#defaultBackoffMs;
 1414 | |                   this.#markCredentialBlocked(args.providerKey, selection.index, blockedUntil);
 1415 | |                   blocked = true;
 1416 | |               }
 1417 | |               const windows = usage ? strategy.findWindowLimits(usage) : undefined;
 1418 | |               const primary = windows?.primary;
 1419 | |               const secondary = windows?.secondary;
 1420 | |               const secondaryTarget = secondary ?? primary;
 1421 | |               ranked.push({
 1422 | |                   selection,
 1423 | |                   usage,
 1424 | |                   usageChecked,
 1425 | |                   blocked,
 1426 | |                   blockedUntil,
 1427 | |                   hasPriorityBoost: strategy.hasPriorityBoost?.(primary) ?? false,
 1428 | |                   secondaryUsed: this.#normalizeUsageFraction(secondaryTarget),
 1429 | |                   secondaryDrainRate: this.#computeWindowDrainRate(
 1430 | |                       secondaryTarget,
 1431 | |                       nowMs,
 1432 | |                       strategy.windowDefaults.secondaryMs,
 1433 | |                   ),
 1434 | |                   primaryUsed: this.#normalizeUsageFraction(primary),
 1435 | |                   primaryDrainRate: this.#computeWindowDrainRate(primary, nowMs, strategy.windowDefaults.primaryMs),
 1436 | |                   orderPos,
 1437 | |               });
 1438 | |           }
 1439 | |           ranked.sort((left, right) => {
 1440 | |               if (left.blocked !== right.blocked) return left.blocked ? 1 : -1;
 1441 | |               if (left.blocked && right.blocked) {
 1442 | |                   const leftBlockedUntil = left.blockedUntil ?? Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
 1443 | |                   const rightBlockedUntil = right.blockedUntil ?? Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
 1444 | |                   if (leftBlockedUntil !== rightBlockedUntil) return leftBlockedUntil - rightBlockedUntil;
 1445 | |                   return left.orderPos - right.orderPos;
 1446 | |               }
 1447 | |               if (requiresOpenAICodexProModel(args.provider, args.options?.modelId)) {
 1448 | |                   const leftPlanPriority = getOpenAICodexPlanPriority(left.usage);
 1449 | |                   const rightPlanPriority = getOpenAICodexPlanPriority(right.usage);
 1450 | |                   if (leftPlanPriority !== rightPlanPriority) return leftPlanPriority - rightPlanPriority;
 1451 | |               }
 1452 | |               if (left.hasPriorityBoost !== right.hasPriorityBoost) return left.hasPriorityBoost ? -1 : 1;
 1453 | |               if (left.secondaryDrainRate !== right.secondaryDrainRate)
 1454 | |                   return left.secondaryDrainRate - right.secondaryDrainRate;
 1455 | |               if (left.secondaryUsed !== right.secondaryUsed) return left.secondaryUsed - right.secondaryUsed;
 1456 | |               if (left.primaryDrainRate !== right.primaryDrainRate) return left.primaryDrainRate - right.primaryDrainRate;
 1457 | |               if (left.primaryUsed !== right.primaryUsed) return left.primaryUsed - right.primaryUsed;
 1458 | |               return left.orderPos - right.orderPos;
 1459 | |           });
 1460 | |           return ranked.map(candidate => ({
 1461 | |               selection: candidate.selection,
 1462 | |               usage: candidate.usage,
 1463 | |               usageChecked: candidate.usageChecked,
 1464 | |           }));
 1465 | |       }
 1466 | |   
 1467 | |       /**
 1468 | |        * Resolves an OAuth API key, trying credentials in priority order.
 1469 | |        * Skips blocked credentials and checks usage limits for providers with usage data.
 1470 | |        * Falls back to earliest-unblocking credential if all are blocked.
 1471 | |        */
 1472 | |       async #resolveOAuthApiKey(
 1473 | |           provider: string,
 1474 | |           sessionId?: string,
 1475 | |           options?: AuthApiKeyOptions,
 1476 | |       ): Promise<string | undefined> {
 1477 | |           const credentials = this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)
 1478 | |               .map((credential, index) => ({ credential, index }))
 1479 | |               .filter((entry): entry is { credential: OAuthCredential; index: number } => entry.credential.type === "oauth");
 1480 | |   
 1481 | |           if (credentials.length === 0) return undefined;
 1482 | |   
 1483 | |           const providerKey = this.#getProviderTypeKey(provider, "oauth");
 1484 | |           const order = this.#getCredentialOrder(providerKey, sessionId, credentials.length);
 1485 | |           const strategy = this.#rankingStrategyResolver?.(provider);
 1486 | |           const requiresProModel = requiresOpenAICodexProModel(provider, options?.modelId);
 1487 | |           const checkUsage = strategy !== undefined && (credentials.length > 1 || requiresProModel);
 1488 | |           const sessionCredential = this.#getSessionCredential(provider, sessionId);
 1489 | |           const sessionPreferredIndex = sessionCredential?.type === "oauth" ? sessionCredential.index : undefined;
 1490 | |           // Skip ranking only when the session already has a working preferred credential — re-ranking
 1491 | |           // mid-session causes account switches that cold-start the server-side prompt cache. New sessions
 1492 | |           // (no preference) and sessions whose preferred is blocked still rank, so we pick the account
 1493 | |           // with the most headroom proactively and fall back intelligently when rate-limited.
 1494 | |           const sessionPreferredIsAvailable =
 1495 | |               sessionPreferredIndex !== undefined && !this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, sessionPreferredIndex);
 1496 | |           const shouldRank = checkUsage && (!sessionPreferredIsAvailable || requiresProModel);
 1497 | |           const candidates = shouldRank
 1498 | |               ? await this.#rankOAuthSelections({ providerKey, provider, order, credentials, options, strategy: strategy! })
 1499 | |               : order
 1500 | |                       .map(idx => credentials[idx])
 1501 | |                       .filter((selection): selection is { credential: OAuthCredential; index: number } => Boolean(selection))
 1502 | |                       .map(selection => ({ selection, usage: null, usageChecked: false }));
 1503 | |   
 1504 | |           if (sessionPreferredIndex !== undefined && !requiresProModel) {
 1505 | |               const sessionPreferredCandidate = candidates.findIndex(
 1506 | |                   candidate =>
 1507 | |                       !this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, candidate.selection.index) &&
 1508 | |                       candidate.selection.index === sessionPreferredIndex,
 1509 | |               );
 1510 | |               if (sessionPreferredCandidate > 0) {
 1511 | |                   const [preferred] = candidates.splice(sessionPreferredCandidate, 1);
 1512 | |                   candidates.unshift(preferred);
 1513 | |               }
 1514 | |           }
 1515 | |           await Promise.all(
 1516 | |               candidates.map(async candidate => {
 1517 | |                   if (Date.now() < candidate.selection.credential.expires) return;
 1518 | |                   const latestCredential = this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider)[candidate.selection.index];
 1519 | |                   if (latestCredential?.type === "oauth" && Date.now() < latestCredential.expires) {
 1520 | |                       candidate.selection.credential = latestCredential;
 1521 | |                       return;
 1522 | |                   }
 1523 | |                   try {
 1524 | |                       const refreshedCredentials = await this.#refreshOAuthCredential(
 1525 | |                           provider,
 1526 | |                           candidate.selection.credential,
 1527 | |                       );
 1528 | |                       candidate.selection.credential = {
 1529 | |                           ...candidate.selection.credential,
 1530 | |                           ...refreshedCredentials,
 1531 | |                           type: "oauth",
 1532 | |                       };
 1533 | |                   } catch {}
 1534 | |               }),
 1535 | |           );
 1536 | |   
 1537 | |           // Skip the Pro-plan filter when no candidate is confirmed Pro, so users with only
 1538 | |           // non-Pro accounts can still attempt Spark requests (e.g. trial/grandfathered access).
 1539 | |           const enforceProRequirement =
 1540 | |               requiresProModel && candidates.some(candidate => hasOpenAICodexProPlan(candidate.usage));
 1541 | |   
 1542 | |           const fallback = candidates[0];
 1543 | |   
 1544 | |           for (const candidate of candidates) {
 1545 | |               const apiKey = await this.#tryOAuthCredential(provider, candidate.selection, providerKey, sessionId, options, {
 1546 | |                   checkUsage,
 1547 | |                   allowBlocked: false,
 1548 | |                   prefetchedUsage: candidate.usage,
 1549 | |                   usagePrechecked: candidate.usageChecked,
 1550 | |                   enforceProRequirement,
 1551 | |               });
 1552 | |               if (apiKey !== null && apiKey !== undefined && apiKey !== "") return apiKey;
 1553 | |           }
 1554 | |   
 1555 | |           if (fallback !== undefined && this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, fallback.selection.index)) {
 1556 | |               return this.#tryOAuthCredential(provider, fallback.selection, providerKey, sessionId, options, {
 1557 | |                   checkUsage,
 1558 | |                   allowBlocked: true,
 1559 | |                   prefetchedUsage: fallback.usage,
 1560 | |                   usagePrechecked: fallback.usageChecked,
 1561 | |                   enforceProRequirement,
 1562 | |               });
 1563 | |           }
 1564 | |   
 1565 | |           return undefined;
 1566 | |       }
 1567 | |   
 1568 | |       async #refreshOAuthCredential(provider: Provider, credential: OAuthCredential): Promise<OAuthCredentials> {
 1569 | |           if (Date.now() < credential.expires) return credential;
 1570 | |           const customProvider = getOAuthProvider(provider);
 1571 | |           let refreshPromise: Promise<OAuthCredentials>;
 1572 | |           if (customProvider !== null && customProvider !== undefined) {
 1573 | |               if (customProvider.refreshToken === null || customProvider.refreshToken === undefined) {
 1574 | |                   throw new Error(`OAuth provider "${provider}" does not support token refresh`);
 1575 | |               }
 1576 | |               refreshPromise = customProvider.refreshToken(credential);
 1577 | |           } else {
 1578 | |               refreshPromise = refreshOAuthToken(provider as OAuthProvider, credential);
 1579 | |           }
 1580 | |           // Bound the refresh so a slow/hanging token endpoint cannot stall credential selection.
 1581 | |           let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout | undefined;
 1582 | |           const timeoutPromise = new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {
 1583 | |               timeout = setTimeout(
 1584 | |                   () => reject(new Error(`OAuth token refresh timed out for provider: ${provider}`)),
 1585 | |                   DEFAULT_OAUTH_REFRESH_TIMEOUT_MS,
 1586 | |               );
 1587 | |           });
 1588 | |           try {
 1589 | |               return await Promise.race([refreshPromise, timeoutPromise]);
 1590 | |           } finally {
 1591 | |               if (timeout) clearTimeout(timeout);
 1592 | |           }
 1593 | |       }
 1594 | |   
 1595 | |       /** Attempts to use a single OAuth credential, checking usage and refreshing token. */
 1596 | |       async #tryOAuthCredential(
 1597 | |           provider: Provider,
 1598 | |           selection: { credential: OAuthCredential; index: number },
 1599 | |           providerKey: string,
 1600 | |           sessionId: string | undefined,
 1601 | |           options: AuthApiKeyOptions | undefined,
 1602 | |           usageOptions: {
 1603 | |               checkUsage: boolean;
 1604 | |               allowBlocked: boolean;
 1605 | |               prefetchedUsage?: UsageReport | null;
 1606 | |               usagePrechecked?: boolean;
 1607 | |               enforceProRequirement?: boolean;
 1608 | |           },
 1609 | |       ): Promise<string | undefined> {
 1610 | |           const {
 1611 | |               checkUsage,
 1612 | |               allowBlocked,
 1613 | |               prefetchedUsage = null,
 1614 | |               usagePrechecked = false,
 1615 | |               enforceProRequirement,
 1616 | |           } = usageOptions;
 1617 | |           if (!allowBlocked && this.#isCredentialBlocked(providerKey, selection.index)) {
 1618 | |               return undefined;
 1619 | |           }
 1620 | |   
 1621 | |           const requiresProModel = requiresOpenAICodexProModel(provider, options?.modelId);
 1622 | |           const applyProFilter = enforceProRequirement ?? requiresProModel;
 1623 | |           let usage: UsageReport | null = null;
 1624 | |           let usageChecked = false;
 1625 | |   
 1626 | |           if ((checkUsage && !allowBlocked) || requiresProModel) {
 1627 | |               if (usagePrechecked) {
 1628 | |                   usage = prefetchedUsage;
 1629 | |               } else {
 1630 | |                   usage = await this.#getUsageReport(provider, selection.credential, {
 1631 | |                       ...options,
 1632 | |                       timeoutMs: this.#usageRequestTimeoutMs,
 1633 | |                   });
 1634 | |               }
 1635 | |               usageChecked = true;
 1636 | |   
 1637 | |               if (applyProFilter && !hasOpenAICodexProPlan(usage)) {
 1638 | |                   return undefined;
 1639 | |               }
 1640 | |               if (checkUsage && !allowBlocked && usage && this.#isUsageLimitReached(usage)) {
 1641 | |                   const resetAtMs = this.#getUsageResetAtMs(usage, Date.now());
 1642 | |                   this.#markCredentialBlocked(
 1643 | |                       providerKey,
 1644 | |                       selection.index,
 1645 | |                       resetAtMs ?? Date.now() + AuthStorage.#defaultBackoffMs,
 1646 | |                   );
 1647 | |                   return undefined;
 1648 | |               }
 1649 | |           }
 1650 | |   
 1651 | |           try {
 1652 | |               let result: { newCredentials: OAuthCredentials; apiKey: string } | null;
 1653 | |               const customProvider = getOAuthProvider(provider);
 1654 | |               if (customProvider !== null && customProvider !== undefined) {
 1655 | |                   const refreshedCredentials = await this.#refreshOAuthCredential(provider, selection.credential);
 1656 | |                   const apiKey =
 1657 | |                       customProvider.getApiKey === null || customProvider.getApiKey === undefined
 1658 | |                           ? refreshedCredentials.access
 1659 | |                           : customProvider.getApiKey(refreshedCredentials);
 1660 | |                   result = { newCredentials: refreshedCredentials, apiKey };
 1661 | |               } else {
 1662 | |                   const oauthCreds: Record<string, OAuthCredentials> = {
 1663 | |                       [provider]: selection.credential,
 1664 | |                   };
 1665 | |                   result = await getOAuthApiKey(provider as OAuthProvider, oauthCreds);
 1666 | |               }
 1667 | |               if (!result) return undefined;
 1668 | |               const updated: OAuthCredential = {
 1669 | |                   type: "oauth",
 1670 | |                   access: result.newCredentials.access,
 1671 | |                   refresh: result.newCredentials.refresh,
 1672 | |                   expires: result.newCredentials.expires,
 1673 | |                   accountId: result.newCredentials.accountId ?? selection.credential.accountId,
 1674 | |                   email: result.newCredentials.email ?? selection.credential.email,
 1675 | |                   projectId: result.newCredentials.projectId ?? selection.credential.projectId,
 1676 | |                   enterpriseUrl: result.newCredentials.enterpriseUrl ?? selection.credential.enterpriseUrl,
 1677 | |               };
 1678 | |               this.#replaceCredentialAt(provider, selection.index, updated);
 1679 | |               if ((checkUsage && !allowBlocked) || requiresProModel) {
 1680 | |                   const sameAccount = selection.credential.accountId === updated.accountId;
 1681 | |                   if (!usageChecked || !sameAccount) {
 1682 | |                       usage = await this.#getUsageReport(provider, updated, {
 1683 | |                           ...options,
 1684 | |                           timeoutMs: this.#usageRequestTimeoutMs,
 1685 | |                       });
 1686 | |                       usageChecked = true;
 1687 | |                   }
 1688 | |                   if (applyProFilter && !hasOpenAICodexProPlan(usage)) {
 1689 | |                       return undefined;
 1690 | |                   }
 1691 | |                   if (checkUsage && !allowBlocked && usage && this.#isUsageLimitReached(usage)) {
 1692 | |                       const resetAtMs = this.#getUsageResetAtMs(usage, Date.now());
 1693 | |                       this.#markCredentialBlocked(
 1694 | |                           providerKey,
 1695 | |                           selection.index,
 1696 | |                           resetAtMs ?? Date.now() + AuthStorage.#defaultBackoffMs,
 1697 | |                       );
 1698 | |                       return undefined;
 1699 | |                   }
 1700 | |               }
 1701 | |               this.#recordSessionCredential(provider, sessionId, "oauth", selection.index);
 1702 | |               return result.apiKey;
 1703 | |           } catch (error) {
 1704 | |               const errorMsg = String(error);
 1705 | |               // Only remove credentials for definitive auth failures
 1706 | |               // Keep credentials for transient errors (network, 5xx) and block temporarily
 1707 | |               const isDefinitiveFailure =
 1708 | |                   /invalid_grant|invalid_token|revoked|unauthorized|expired.*refresh|refresh.*expired/i.test(errorMsg) ||
 1709 | |                   (/\b(401|403)\b/.test(errorMsg) && !/timeout|network|fetch failed|ECONNREFUSED/i.test(errorMsg));
 1710 | |   
 1711 | |               logger.warn("OAuth token refresh failed", {
 1712 | |                   provider,
 1713 | |                   index: selection.index,
 1714 | |                   error: errorMsg,
 1715 | |                   isDefinitiveFailure,
 1716 | |               });
 1717 | |   
 1718 | |               if (isDefinitiveFailure) {
 1719 | |                   // Permanently disable invalid credentials with an explicit cause for inspection/debugging
 1720 | |                   this.#disableCredentialAt(provider, selection.index, `oauth refresh failed: ${errorMsg}`);
 1721 | |                   if (this.#getCredentialsForProvider(provider).some(credential => credential.type === "oauth")) {
 1722 | |                       return this.getApiKey(provider, sessionId, options);
 1723 | |                   }
 1724 | |               } else {
 1725 | |                   // Block temporarily for transient failures (5 minutes)
 1726 | |                   this.#markCredentialBlocked(providerKey, selection.index, Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000);
 1727 | |               }
 1728 | |           }
 1729 | |   
 1730 | |           return undefined;
 1731 | |       }
 1732 | |   
 1733 | |       /**
 1734 | |        * Peek at API key for a provider without refreshing OAuth tokens.
 1735 | |        * Used for model discovery where we only need to know if credentials exist
 1736 | |        * and get a best-effort token.
 1737 | |        */
 1738 | |       async peekApiKey(provider: string): Promise<string | undefined> {
 1739 | |           const runtimeKey = this.#runtimeOverrides.get(provider);
 1740 | |           if (runtimeKey !== null && runtimeKey !== undefined && runtimeKey !== "") {
 1741 | |               return runtimeKey;
 1742 | |           }
 1743 | |   
 1744 | |           const apiKeySelection = this.#selectCredentialByType(provider, "api_key");
 1745 | |           if (apiKeySelection) {
 1746 | |               return this.#configValueResolver(apiKeySelection.credential.key);
 1747 | |           }
 1748 | |   
 1749 | |           // Return current OAuth access token only if it is not already expired.
 1750 | |           const oauthSelection = this.#selectCredentialByType(provider, "oauth");
 1751 | |           if (oauthSelection) {
 1752 | |               const expiresAt = oauthSelection.credential.expires;
 1753 | |               if (Number.isFinite(expiresAt) && expiresAt > Date.now()) {
 1754 | |                   return oauthSelection.credential.access;
 1755 | |               }
 1756 | |           }
 1757 | |   
 1758 | |           const envKey = getEnvApiKey(provider);
 1759 | |           if (envKey !== null && envKey !== undefined && envKey !== "") return envKey;
 1760 | |   
 1761 | |           return this.#fallbackResolver?.(provider) ?? undefined;
 1762 | |       }
 1763 | |   
 1764 | |       /**
 1765 | |        * Get API key for a provider.
 1766 | |        * Priority:
 1767 | |        * 1. Runtime override (CLI --api-key)
 1768 | |        * 2. API key from storage
 1769 | |        * 3. OAuth token from storage (auto-refreshed)
 1770 | |        * 4. Environment variable
 1771 | |        * 5. Fallback resolver (models.json custom providers)
 1772 | |        */
 1773 | |       async getApiKey(provider: string, sessionId?: string, options?: AuthApiKeyOptions): Promise<string | undefined> {
 1774 | |           // Runtime override takes highest priority
 1775 | |           const runtimeKey = this.#runtimeOverrides.get(provider);
 1776 | |           if (runtimeKey !== null && runtimeKey !== undefined && runtimeKey !== "") {
 1777 | |               return runtimeKey;
 1778 | |           }
 1779 | |   
 1780 | |           const apiKeySelection = this.#selectCredentialByType(provider, "api_key", sessionId);
 1781 | |           if (apiKeySelection) {
 1782 | |               this.#recordSessionCredential(provider, sessionId, "api_key", apiKeySelection.index);
 1783 | |               return this.#configValueResolver(apiKeySelection.credential.key);
 1784 | |           }
 1785 | |   
 1786 | |           const oauthKey = await this.#resolveOAuthApiKey(provider, sessionId, options);
 1787 | |           if (oauthKey !== null && oauthKey !== undefined && oauthKey !== "") {
 1788 | |               return oauthKey;
 1789 | |           }
 1790 | |   
 1791 | |           // Fall back to environment variable
 1792 | |           const envKey = getEnvApiKey(provider);
 1793 | |           if (envKey !== null && envKey !== undefined && envKey !== "") return envKey;
 1794 | |   
 1795 | |           // Fall back to custom resolver (e.g., models.json custom providers)
 1796 | |           return this.#fallbackResolver?.(provider) ?? undefined;
 1797 | |       }
